With this app, you don’t have to guess what information is being collected from your device. \r\n\r\n    How does Diagnostic Data Viewer work? \r\n\r\n    - Immediately see the diagnostic data that Microsoft collects from your device in real-time, exactly the way it appears when it is sent \r\n    - If you’ve chosen Basic for your privacy settings, see that Microsoft collects only the data required to help keep your Windows device up-to-date and secure. \r\n    - If you’ve opted into Full, see that Microsoft collects from your device diagnostic data that helps improve our products and services to make the Windows experience better for everyone.  \r\n\r\n    To help improve future releases of this app, the app also collects general usage and startup problem data.
